If there are 739 girls How many boys are there in that school?", "answer": "( 739.0 - 402.0 )=337.0", "output1": " Step 1: Let X be the number of boys in the school, then the number of girls is X+<<+402=402>>402\nStep 2: The total number of students in the school is X+(X+402)=739\nStep 3: 2*X + 402 = 739\nStep 4: 2*X = 739-402\nStep 5: 2*X = 337\nStep 6: Then the number of boys is X = 337/2\nStep 7: There are <<338=338>>338 boys in the school.\nanswer: 338", "cnt_step": 7, "output2": ["Step 1 is all correct.", "Step 2 is all correct.", "Step 3 is wrong.", "Step 4 is all correct.", "Step 5 is all correct.", "Step 6 is all correct.", "Step 7 is wrong."], "pred_wrong_step": 3, "output3": "Step 1: Let X be the number of boys in the school.
